  736 |  2   FDRAW.LINE.s     73 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/8D38               | * We use a traditional Bresenham run-length approach.
  737 |  2   FDRAW.LINE.s     74 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/8D38               | * Run-slicing is possible, but the code is larger
  738 |  2   FDRAW.LINE.s     75 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/8D38               | * and the increased cost means it's only valuable
  739 |  2   FDRAW.LINE.s     76 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/8D38               | * for longer lines.  An optimal solution would switch
  740 |  2   FDRAW.LINE.s     77 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/8D38               | * approaches based on line length.
  741 |  2   FDRAW.LINE.s     78 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/8D38               | *
  742 |  2   FDRAW.LINE.s     79 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/8D38               | * Start by identifying where x0 or x1 is on the
  743 |  2   FDRAW.LINE.s     80 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/8D38               | * left.  To make life simpler we always work from
  744 |  2   FDRAW.LINE.s     81 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/8D38               | * left to right, flipping the coordinates if
  745 |  2   FDRAW.LINE.s     82 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/8D38               | * needed.
  746 |  2   FDRAW.LINE.s     83 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/8D38               | *
  747 |  2   FDRAW.LINE.s     84 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/8D38               | * We also need to figure out if the line is more
  748 |  2   FDRAW.LINE.s     85 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/8D38               | * than 255 pixels long -- which, because of
  749 |  2   FDRAW.LINE.s     86 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/8D38               | * inclusive coordinates, means abs(x0-x1) > 254.
  750 |  2   FDRAW.LINE.s     87 | Code        | 11 |         |    3 | 00/8D38 : AD 09 8A    |                 lda   in_x1l         ;assume x0 on left
  751 |  2   FDRAW.LINE.s     88 | Code        | 11 |         |    1 | 00/8D3B : 38          |                 sec                  
  752 |  2   FDRAW.LINE.s     89 | Code        | 11 |         |    3 | 00/8D3C : ED 06 8A    |                 sbc   in_x0l         
  753 |  2   FDRAW.LINE.s     90 | Code        | 11 |         |    1 | 00/8D3F : AA          |                 tax                  
  754 |  2   FDRAW.LINE.s     91 | Code        | 11 |         |    2 | 00/8D40 : F0 2D       |                 beq   checkvert      ;low bytes even, check hi
  755 |  2   FDRAW.LINE.s     92 | Code        | 11 |         |    3 | 00/8D42 : AD 0A 8A    |                 lda   in_x1h

 2067 |  4 FDRAW.TABLES.s    200 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/99C6               | * RastFill unrolled loop.  At each step we store the current
 2068 |  4 FDRAW.TABLES.s    201 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/99C6               | * color value, XOR it to flip the bits if needed, and advance.
 2069 |  4 FDRAW.TABLES.s    202 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/99C6               | * The caller needs to set the appropriate initial value based
 2070 |  4 FDRAW.TABLES.s    203 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/99C6               | * on whether the address is odd or even.
 2071 |  4 FDRAW.TABLES.s    204 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/99C6               | *
 2072 |  4 FDRAW.TABLES.s    205 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/99C6               | * We can use a 3-cycle "EOR dp" or a 2-cycle "EOR imm".  The
 2073 |  4 FDRAW.TABLES.s    206 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/99C6               | * former is one cycle slower, the latter requires us to
 2074 |  4 FDRAW.TABLES.s    207 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/99C6               | * self-mod 40 instructions when the color changes.
 2075 |  4 FDRAW.TABLES.s    208 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/99C6               | *
 2076 |  4 FDRAW.TABLES.s    209 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/99C6               | * This must be page-aligned so that we can take the value
 2077 |  4 FDRAW.TABLES.s    210 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/99C6               | * from the rastunidx table and self-mod a JMP without having
 2078 |  4 FDRAW.TABLES.s    211 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/99C6               | * to do a 16-bit add.  We have just enough room for the
 2079 |  4 FDRAW.TABLES.s    212 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/99C6               | * unrolled loop (40*5+3) and x5 table (41) = 244 bytes, fits
 2080 |  4 FDRAW.TABLES.s    213 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/99C6               | * on a single page.
